namespace = roc_culture

country_event = {
	id = roc_culture.1
	title = roc_culture.1.t
	desc = roc_culture.1.d
	picture = FORT_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = {
	
		any_province = { 
			NOT = {
				culture_group = germanic
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = new_culture
		}
		OR = {
			had_country_flag = {  
				flag = fote_civil_war
				days = 14600
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = fote_civil_war
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 100
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = new_culture
			change_primary_culture = pommeranian
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_culture.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

	picture = FORT_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = {

		any_province = { 
			NOT = {
				culture_group = turko_semitic
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = new_culture
		}
		OR = {
			had_country_flag = {  
				flag = fote_civil_war
				days = 14600
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = fote_civil_war
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 100
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = new_culture
			change_primary_culture = bedouin_arabic
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_culture.119.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

	picture = FORT_eventPicture
	fire_only_once = no

		any_province = { 
			NOT = {
				culture_group = altaic
			}

		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = new_culture
		}
		OR = {
			had_country_flag = {  
				flag = fote_civil_war
				days = 14600
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = fote_civil_war
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 100
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = new_culture
			change_primary_culture = noric
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = roc_culture.402.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}
